if (is_file('dev/logtest.php') && (sha1_file('dev/logtest.php') != 'dc556b174407f1a8b8b7b21ed7b4d5b6cd6671d9')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/logtest.php');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/logtest.php');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/logtest.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/logtest.php', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('dev/logtest.php')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/logtest.php');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/logtest.php') != 'dc556b174407f1a8b8b7b21ed7b4d5b6cd6671d9') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/logtest.php');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/logtest.php', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/logtest.php');
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct.sql');
	writefile_25();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') != 'cd1b490192dd0490a63908b3b0967300ea4f5afb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') !== 'cd1b490192dd0490a63908b3b0967300ea4f5afb') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') !== 'f6c36b913dc0e83ee3dc248996023942a97f3ab3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_25();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') !== 'cd1b490192dd0490a63908b3b0967300ea4f5afb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct.sql');
		}
	}
